# Tiny Tina's Wonderlands
#
# This seems to be nearly complete, though it's missing more name mappings
# than Borderlands 3.  Of the 9,096 .txtp files generated, 328 of them are
# missing the primary label (about 3%).  I blame that on not having an
# unstripped Mac binary to pull more names from, though I did include a
# dump of memory when constructing the initial list.
#
# There's also a nonzero amount of incorrect names here, on account of
# hash collisions (but not having the "real" name in the list to make it
# obvious).  `NtGdiGetAppliedDeviceGammaRam2 {r}.txtp`, etc.  C'est la vie!
#
# The script used to generate the initial list (which was then pared down
# to produce this list) can be found here:
#
# https://github.com/apocalyptech/wldata/blob/master/gen_initial_wwnames.py
